  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_86816007-505b-4a6a-884b-226d143c191c'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText17891844856588986850" style="display:none">Corrado Moretti.<br /><br />The world knows the notorious Kevlar Killer, but few have ever seen what lies beneath his armor. The abused child. The neglected teenager. The broken man. He always did whatever he had to do in order to survive.<br /><br />It's kill or be killed.<br /><br />Throughout his life, he has been there in the shadows, a witness to everything from beginning to end. Bound by loyalty and honor, there's only one thing he would sacrifice it all for: family.<br /><br />Never get close. Never get attached. It's a lesson that has been brutally pounded into him since childhood, but they're words the DeMarcos make it difficult for him to follow. Through them he finds love and grieves loss, realizing the world isn't quite as black and white as it's made out to be.<br /><br />Made.</span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });
      $('span_class_gr-hyperlink_sort_order_span_tip_665').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>    </div>
</div>

<div id="review_1069637971" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1069637971" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1069637971?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1069637971" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer958553484253420505"><b>5+ Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/71a66155-5496-4851-ac07-c236f1239448_zpsb49856f4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414519825i/11662368.jpg' alt=' photo 71a66155-5496-4851-ac07-c236f1239448_zpsb49856f4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After reading the <i>Sempre</i> books, I knew I wanted to know more about Corrado Morretti. There was just something about him… When I heard we were getting a Corrado book, I was ecstatic. It did not disappoint! In fact, it exceeded all my expectations. This book was fantastic. It will be going right towards the top of my favorites list for this year. <br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"What made you this way?" <br/>"Sweetheart, I wouldn't even know where to begin.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><b>MADE</b> is the story of Corrado Morretti. From his ch</span>
  <span id="freeText958553484253420505" style="display:none"><b>5+ Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/71a66155-5496-4851-ac07-c236f1239448_zpsb49856f4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414519825i/11662368.jpg" alt=" photo 71a66155-5496-4851-ac07-c236f1239448_zpsb49856f4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After reading the <i>Sempre</i> books, I knew I wanted to know more about Corrado Morretti. There was just something about him… When I heard we were getting a Corrado book, I was ecstatic. It did not disappoint! In fact, it exceeded all my expectations. This book was fantastic. It will be going right towards the top of my favorites list for this year. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"What made you this way?" <br>"Sweetheart, I wouldn't even know where to begin.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><b>MADE</b> is the story of Corrado Morretti. From his childhood, to teenage years, to adulthood. We get it all. The entire story. <br><br>Corrado’s childhood was not easy to read about. He learned from an early age how to take care of himself. The way the world worked. With an abusive mother, manipulative sister and absent father, it wasn’t easy. Corrado saw the work his father did with La Costa Nostra from a young age. It was a normal thing for him. Corrado learned to keep to himself, not to feel, not to form attachments. Until he meets a child named Celia DeMarco that is. When she comes back into his life when he’s a little older (maybe 19) everything changes.<br><b>
  <blockquote>He'd certainly met his match with her.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/87212bf3-b5bd-4271-b30e-ba1b8d9fe32e_zps0ac37d58.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414519825i/11662369.jpg" alt=" photo 87212bf3-b5bd-4271-b30e-ba1b8d9fe32e_zps0ac37d58.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Corrado is just finding his place in La Costa Nostra, where Celia’s father is the boss. Corrado’s feelings for Celia come back full force. She wants to be with him too… but he’s not sure if it’s possible. Celia is full of love and life. Quite the opposite of Corrado in a lot of ways. She trys to convince him otherwise. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"I know how to keep a secret," she said. "That's in my blood, too. And I know without a doubt that you know how, too. He wouldn't even have to know." <br><br>"You're worth more than that," Corrado said. "You deserve to be somebody's everything, not somebody's secret.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Eventually, they are able to work things out with the boss. <br>The romance between Corrado and Celia was beautiful. If you ever think that someone that does the kind of work Corrado does can’t have true love, can’t be loyal and loving, you’re wrong. I especially loved that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Celia is the only woman he’s ever been with… swoon! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/d1d2bdaa-2852-4091-9df0-f25c1bd113c1_zps10d5e1b6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414519825i/11662370.jpg" alt=" photo d1d2bdaa-2852-4091-9df0-f25c1bd113c1_zps10d5e1b6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There are a few parts of Corrado and Celia’s relationship that hurt my heart. Like the baby thing. I really felt for Celia, though I could sympathize with Corrado. With all he sees and the way he grew up. <br><br>We all know Corrado is a badass, but the way he was so sweet and swoony with Celia- I loved it! He might not have been the most traditional husband, but it’s the thought that counts. I laughed every time he brought her flowers. No matter what was going on in his life, Corrado never lost the love he had for Celia. Never looked at anyone else. He never strayed. Besides the job, she was his life. His reason for being. If thats not the most romantic thing, I don’t know what is. <br><i>
  <blockquote>"It's the way you're looking at me... it's like you've never seen something so beautiful before."<br><br>"I haven't."<br><br>"That's the way you're looking at me."<br><br>"And it bothers you?"<br><br>"I cant' live up to it. You put me on a pedestal. I'll only fall."<br><br>"You'll never fall. Not if I'm there to catch you." </blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/cef59e56-137b-4c2f-a900-edb1208cdc64_zps02743d76.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414519825i/11662371.jpg" alt=" photo cef59e56-137b-4c2f-a900-edb1208cdc64_zps02743d76.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Corrado was logical and thorough in his work. He didn’t think about the people, he thought about the job. Thats what it was to him. Just a job. Kill or be killed. Sink or swim. Corrado was always the killer, always the man swimming. Indestructible. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"The world made me this way. And maybe they all hate me, but still, they need me. Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes." </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/e7bc8876-60f1-4574-beb8-ecbb138d241e_zps4f7fafee.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414519825i/11662372.jpg" alt=" photo e7bc8876-60f1-4574-beb8-ecbb138d241e_zps4f7fafee.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>His nickname was great. This book is more of a mafia book than the <i>Sempre</i> books. You’ll notice that Corrado is in much deeper than the DeMarco boys (Vincent and Carmine) ever were. I did enjoy getting the Vincent and Maura story. It was nice to see how that came about. You see a whole different side of Vincent as well. <br><br>I can’t think of one thing I didn’t love about this story. Getting to read about Corrado Morretti… it was perfect. Just so readers know, you technically don’t have to read the <i>Sempre</i> books to read this, but I highly recommend that you do. I think you’d get so much more out of this story. Plus, if you ever go back and read <i>Sempre</i> after this, there would be so much spoiled. <br><br>It’s no secret that I love <i>Sempre</i> and her <i>Monster</i> books, so for me to say that this is JM Darhower’s best book is a big deal. The writing was stellar. It’s a long book, but it doesn't feel long. It was so fast paced and captivating I didn’t realize I had been reading for hours until I looked up at the clock. <br><br>Even though Corrado Morretti is a ruthless killer, there is something about the way he loves his woman completely and eternally that makes him so beautiful and lovable. I just couldn’t get enough of Corrado and Celia’s story. I’m so grateful that JM Darhower decided to write this story and I can’t recommend it enough! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/235c3b51-5aff-4a83-aae2-cc41e82b21f2_zpsb602de83.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414519825i/11662373.jpg" alt=" photo 235c3b51-5aff-4a83-aae2-cc41e82b21f2_zpsb602de83.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/fbfe5257-5c23-4da3-b325-31eaf8f2110a_zpsd0802295.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399922023i/9610271.jpg" alt=" photo fbfe5257-5c23-4da3-b325-31eaf8f2110a_zpsd0802295.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <i>“A blush tinged her bronzed skin as she wrapped her arms around herself. Corrado grasped her wrists, pulling her hands away when she tried to shield herself. He stared at her, stunned to see the uncertainty in her eyes.<br/>"You're not nervous this time, </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText177851698381571819" style="display:none"><i>Ps. If you wanna read this series, I suggest you to read with this order otherwise this book will give you major spoilers about Sempre &amp; Sempre:Redemption.<br>* Sempre<br>* Sempre:Redemption<br>* Friends - Novella<br>* Forever - Novella<br>* Made</i><br><br>---------------------<br><br><b>
  <i>“A blush tinged her bronzed skin as she wrapped her arms around herself. Corrado grasped her wrists, pulling her hands away when she tried to shield herself. He stared at her, stunned to see the uncertainty in her eyes.<br>"You're not nervous this time, are you?" he asked, half-teasingly, half honestly wanting to know. She'd been so confident, unwavering before.<br>"It's the way you're looking at me."<br>"How am I looking at you?"<br>"Like you look at the Taj Mahal. Or the Sistine Chapel. You're staring at me like you stare at the Mona Lisa."<br>"I've never seen those things."<br>"It's like you've never seen something so beautiful before."<br>"I haven’t.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491553297ra/22421260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Corrado Alphonse Moretti. I’ll never ever forget you... <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18338465.Sempre__Sempre___1_" title="Sempre (Sempre, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Sempre</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17838379.Redemption__Sempre___2_" title="Redemption (Sempre, #2) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Sempre: Redemption</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23295358.Made__Sempre___0_4_" title="Made (Sempre, #0.4) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Made</a> . Total 1.475 pages – 12 days – God knows how many hours I read these books… It was an unforgettable journey that’s for sure cause this books gave me the best days of my life… They reminded me why I love reading a good book because this books made me to feel every word, every pain of this characters going through… <br><br>I loved all the books in this series. Each one of is beautiful but this book.. My God, this one was something special. Corrado’s love for Celia and their chemistry was amazing… So unique, so pure… <br><br>I laughed a lot when Celia &amp; Corrado together. Because their moments was just so lovely. And I cried so much while I was reading this book. But especially when I read the last chapter of the book and right after that amazing epilogue broke my heart so bad… Ugh I cried and when I start to cried, I just couldn’t stop myself and I cried like a river… And the absurd thing is I was reading that parts in a coffee shop and I cried in public while I read a book and I didn’t even care who looked at me or what people thought… I never in my life cried in public but this book made me and I’m not even sorry for that… Cause this book deserved my every single tears...<br><br><b>
  <i>J.M.Darhower, I love you, I adore you… Thank you very much for this journey! YOU ARE FREAKING AWESOME!!! &lt;3</i>

<div id="review_1305603853" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1305603853" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1305603853?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1305603853" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11427963584222410701">J.M.Darhower...<br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434158491ra/15180155.gif' width='390' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You wrote such an incredible story for Corrado Moretti! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434159216ra/15180190.gif' width='390' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"The world made me this way. And maybe they all hate me, but still, they need me. Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes."</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>If you are looking for that rare five star read that’s writing and storytelling is exceptional then look no further than this book. If you have skipped because you haven’t read the Sempre series and/or completed said series do not hesitate this book can be read as a stand</span>
  <span id="freeText11427963584222410701" style="display:none">J.M.Darhower...<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434158491ra/15180155.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You wrote such an incredible story for Corrado Moretti! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434159216ra/15180190.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"The world made me this way. And maybe they all hate me, but still, they need me. Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes."</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>If you are looking for that rare five star read that’s writing and storytelling is exceptional then look no further than this book. If you have skipped because you haven’t read the Sempre series and/or completed said series do not hesitate this book can be read as a standalone and is by far the author’s best work to date. <br> <br>I simply ADORED fiery Celia DeMarco, young Vincent DeMarco, the Don himself, Antonio DeMarco, Vito Morretti (who may not be the father of the year but fully captured my heart) and of course the Kevlar Killer ~ Corrado Morretti!<br> <br>The story takes Corrado all the way from a hard childhood to the <b>MADE</b> man he is in adulthood. Corrado faces the highs and lows of life, love, family all while being an intricate part of the mafia. I cried on more than one occasion, I laughed, I cringed at the cruelty and I swooned over the love Corrado and Celia share. This is a timeless piece that will now sit on my favorite shelf my only regret being that I didn’t read it sooner. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434391290ra/15215446.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Your light is the only thing in this world not tainted by my darkness."</i>
</b><br></span>

This book. Holy shit. I loved every minute. Seriously, I wanted to do nothing but stay with these characters. These beautifully flawed characters, have earned a special place in my heart. <i>Made</i> was simply a perfect story, IMO, full of heart, family, loyalty - the experience was one I will never forget. <br/><br/>This is one of my favorite Corrado moments -<br/><br/><i>

</i><br><br>Honestly, I can't put into words how much I loved this story. Just read it. Highly recommend this one!<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437072150ra/15535381.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>

<div id="review_1084214828" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1084214828" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1084214828?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=alpha-heroes">alpha-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=pull-out-the-guns-mafia">pull-out-the-guns-mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=this-is-for-ana">this-is-for-ana</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1084214828" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14152736436217412614"><b>5 stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413869948i/11575059._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I could spend days telling you how much I’ve been looking forward to this book so I’ll just go with a simple ‘I’ve been waiting for Corrado Moretti’s story since 2012.’ Not only was he one of my earliest book boyfriends, but he also was the very first guy I’d read about who was in the mafia so needless to say, he has a very special place in my heart. I was surprised that this book was longer than the Sempre books but that made me happy; the more Corrado, the better! This book is like a </span>
  <span id="freeText14152736436217412614" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413869948i/11575059._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I could spend days telling you how much I’ve been looking forward to this book so I’ll just go with a simple ‘I’ve been waiting for Corrado Moretti’s story since 2012.’ Not only was he one of my earliest book boyfriends, but he also was the very first guy I’d read about who was in the mafia so needless to say, he has a very special place in my heart. I was surprised that this book was longer than the Sempre books but that made me happy; the more Corrado, the better! This book is like a chronicle of Corrado’s life and each part is categorized by a major turning point in his life. J.M. Darhower left no stone unturned; from his childhood to teenage years to the Corrado we know him now as is all written down and I lapped it all up. But first, the beginning…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413869948i/11575060._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before Corrado was known as the fearless <i>Kevlar Killer,</i> before he was ever exposed to the harsh mafia world, he was a boy. A lonely, misguided and mistreated boy who suffered from his mother’s physical and emotional abuse and had a father who was always absent. Growing up under these family circumstances, Corrado further isolated himself from what you’d expect normal kids to grow into. And eventually he realizes that he doesn’t fit in. He’s different. The life he currently lives holds no meaning and he has no purpose. Traits like detachment, decisiveness, and cunning all points him in the direction of his father’s ‘career’ path, the mafia. And even though he starts off on shaky ground, Corrado finds his true talents and purpose with mafia work. The adrenaline, the rush of power, the hits all come natural to him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413869948i/11575061._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We’re treated to multiple scenes where Corrado more than proves his worth along with intriguing mafia dynamics and most importantly, his beautiful relationship with Celia, his one and only weakness. In the Sempre books it’s heavily hinted that Corrado and Celia’s marriage was a love match but the one question that plagued me was <i>how?</i> How does one as cold as Corrado and one as bright as Celia fall in love? This book is the answer. Their relationship is anything but predictable and the way their paths cross had me sighing and swooning. I think what makes Corrado more endearing to me than most heroes is that despite the dark, suffocating world he lives in, he hasn’t completely lost his ability to love even though he’s unemotional most of the time. So when a man like him falls, he falls deep and he falls hard. And there isn’t a better girl he could’ve fallen in love with than the vivacious Celia who brings light into his dim world. Normal concerns couples have like cheating, jealousy, etc…are so trivial and petty to him because there will only ever be one woman for him. That one woman who is worth fighting for. Worth killing for. Worth dying for. That kind of love and feeling coming from a ruthless killer just seems to magnify it to epic proportions, at least I think so.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413869948i/11575062._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reading this book hit me hard with the feels. Since this was literally a record of Corrado’s life story, I felt as if I lived through 40 years myself. To go through his childhood, his turbulent teenage years and his rise in the mafia underground and his enduring relationship with Celia, it was like reading a saga. Once I finished the book, I felt an immediate sense of loss and heavily contemplated the legacy of a man who gave nothing and everything, who had to be cruel in order to be kind, and a dozen other contradictions to live the life that chose him. <br><br><u>Made</u> is set in the time before and during the events of <u>Sempre</u> and <u>Sempre-Redemption</u> and can technically be read on its own. However, it also contains major plot spoilers for both Sempre books so I would recommend reading those books first before starting this one. <br><br><i>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14152736436217412614" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1069546732" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1064961045299705227"><b>Sale for $0.99-> </b> <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1wr257Q'>http://amzn.to/1wr257Q</a><br/>12/19/2014<br/><br/><b>Giveaway of this book </b>-><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://bit.ly/1pQNC06'>http://bit.ly/1pQNC06</a><br/><br/>To quote Celia, <b>“Wow. That was… wow.” </b> I loved every single minute of this book. It’s a huge book and yet it didn’t feel long because it was so captivating. <br/><br/><b>MADE</b> is Corrado’s life story. I read <b>SEMPRE</b> in 2012 and fell in love with the story. I was curious about Corrado in that story so when I saw the dedication in MADE I knew this book was for me: <br/><b>To everyone out there who read Sempre and wanted to kno</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1064961045299705227" style="display:none"><b>Sale for $0.99-&gt; </b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1wr257Q">http://amzn.to/1wr257Q</a><br>12/19/2014<br><br><b>Giveaway of this book </b>-&gt;<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1pQNC06">http://bit.ly/1pQNC06</a><br><br>To quote Celia, <b>“Wow. That was… wow.” </b> I loved every single minute of this book. It’s a huge book and yet it didn’t feel long because it was so captivating. <br><br><b>MADE</b> is Corrado’s life story. I read <b>SEMPRE</b> in 2012 and fell in love with the story. I was curious about Corrado in that story so when I saw the dedication in MADE I knew this book was for me: <br><b>To everyone out there who read Sempre and wanted to know more about a certain mysterious hitman. This is for you. </b><br><br><i>Made</i> starts with a reporter asking Corrado,<b> “What made you this way?”</b> To which Corrado replies,<b> “Sweetheart, I wouldn’t even know where to begin.” </b> On the cover of the book Ms. Darhower wrote: <b>Men are what their mothers made them. </b> <br><br><b>Corrado</b> is an enigma that leaves you swooning for him. <i> He’s a man with a gun and no regard for his own life.</i> His quiet strength and desensitized self is a scary combo. The only one who never saw him as a monster was Celia. She loved him from the first moment he spoke. <br><br><b>Celia</b> is a firecracker, full of emotions. Being the bosses daughter she is use to getting what she wants when she wants it. I loved how she’s a strong woman who doesn’t back down to anyone. Her sarcastic humor had me cracking up. The banter between the two of them felt genuine. When Corrado complained about a situation out of their control she had a witty comeback for him, <b> “You’re such a hopeless romantic, Corrado Moretti. It’s amazing more women don’t swoon over you.” </b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414208339i/11623323._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>No sappy romance will be found between the pages of this book. Instead you will find a romance between two characters who love each other deeply and make sacrifices to be together. Their devotion to each other had me swooning. <b>“I’m a lot of things, Celia DeMarco, but I’m not this. I’ll cheat the law, I’ll cheat on my taxes, I’ll try my damnedest to cheat death, but never… never… will I cheat on you.”</b><br><br>J.M. Darhower’s created one of my favorite books of 2014 with this story. I can’t stop thinking about how phenomenal <b>Made</b> was and how this story will stick with me long after I close the pages of the book. So my final advice- <b>READ IT</b>!!!<br><br><b>WAIT</b>: I have one more thing to say that comes from Winnie the Pooh, <b>"How lucky I am to have something that makes saying goodbye so hard."</b> Even though I didn't want their story to end I'm glad I read it. <br><br>✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦<br><b>RELEASE DATE: October 27, 2014 </b><br>Pre-order | order: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1wr257Q">http://amzn.to/1wr257Q</a><br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13111733.Sempre__Forever___1_" title="Sempre (Forever, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1340797919s/13111733.jpg" alt="Sempre (Forever, #1) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17838379.Sempre_Redemption__Forever___2_" title="Sempre Redemption (Forever, #2) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1383420595s/17838379.jpg" alt="Sempre Redemption (Forever, #2) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Continuing story<br><br><i>Novellas:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23295358.Made__Forever___0_4_" title="Made (Forever, #0.4) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1412741893s/23295358.jpg" alt="Made (Forever, #0.4) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23341510.Friends__Forever___0_5_" title="Friends (Forever, #0.5) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1417541821s/23341510.jpg" alt="Friends (Forever, #0.5) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23341511.Forever__Forever___2_5_" title="Forever (Forever, #2.5) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1412742076s/23341511.jpg" alt="Forever (Forever, #2.5) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>Made</b> is connected to the Sempre series, it is NOT a sequel.<b> It is a spin-off prequel and can be as a standalone,</b> although it will contain spoilers for the Sempre books.<br><br>**Complimentary copy in exchange for an honest review.**<br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408724793i/10887518.png" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><b>I met my goal for 2014 with this book!!</b> <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user_challenges/1196247" rel="nofollow noopener">150th book of 2014</a></span>

<div id="review_1069789535" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1069789535" />
    <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review"><img alt="Peek At My Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1414761368p2/18263404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1069789535?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Peek At My Book Review" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review">Peek At My Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Peek At My Book Review by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3991800-none">None</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1069789535" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16492010477575367142"><b>Rating :</b> <b>5 +++ Corrado Alphonse Moretti Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414504683ra/11660756.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>My Views :</b> First I would like to give a Big Sincere Thanks to Jessica Mae Darhower for giving us the pleasure of reading Corrado’s story and write a story for her readers. A story that was not written in haste but to satisfy and please her readers not matter what the length. Corrado couldn’t have a better story than this one.<br/><br/>The book is divided in to different stages of Corrado’s life, starting with his childhood. I was quite shocked to see Katrina as</span>
  <span id="freeText16492010477575367142" style="display:none"><b>Rating :</b> <b>5 +++ Corrado Alphonse Moretti Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414504683ra/11660756.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My Views :</b> First I would like to give a Big Sincere Thanks to Jessica Mae Darhower for giving us the pleasure of reading Corrado’s story and write a story for her readers. A story that was not written in haste but to satisfy and please her readers not matter what the length. Corrado couldn’t have a better story than this one.<br><br>The book is divided in to different stages of Corrado’s life, starting with his childhood. I was quite shocked to see Katrina as a child, even though she already had vileness in her, she was still innocent and I loved the way Corrado looked after her; they had the sisterly and brotherly bond that didn’t take much time to crumble down. <br><b>
  <i> "The more she hates you, the more she likes me."</i>
</b><br><br>There is also a little love story between Corrado and Celia that started when they were still kids, I adore Celia as much as love Corrado, and they are perfect for each other. I just couldn’t stop from visualizing myself as Celia <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414504683ra/11660757.gif" width="45" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then you have Maura and Vincent as side story…Having read the other books and see these characters when they were young, there is so much disparity between now and what they will become. Vincent was another surprise as he is totally different from what he will be and it’s nice to get to know Maura.<br><br><b>Style of writing :</b> Amazing, Miss Darhower has a talent of writing that just captures the reader’s attention. The fact that she gave us Corrado’s life from childhood till adulthood and not even once I felt like I was bored, in fact I refused to sleep, eat and had to hold myself to leakage point to go to pee…Eewww I know, but I just couldn’t put that book down. <br><br><b>
  <i> "It's the way you're looking at me."<br>"How am I looking at you?"<br>"Like you look at the Taj Mahal. Or the Sistine Chapel. You're staring at me like you stare at the Mona Lisa."<br>"I've never seen those things."<br>"It's like you've never seen something so beautiful before."<br>"I haven’t."<br>She shivered at his words. "That's the way you're looking at me."<br>"And that bothers you?"<br>"I can't live up to it," she said. "You can't put me on a pedestal. I'll only fall."<br>"You'll never fall," he said. "Not if I'm there to catch you."</i>
</b><br><br><b>Characters :</b> Oh my God, I have never portrait Celia as someone carefree in the other books but in this one she was wow. She is the one to get Corrado out of his shell and I had no doubt that she would have been the one to initiate the first kiss and other things also, if you see what I mean I’m sure you do. (My God that woman’s quick, Corrado never stood a chance) <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/228438.gif" width="45" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i> After one last kiss, she stepped away, wrapping his jacket tightly around her. "I'm keeping the coat."<br>"Okay."<br>"I'm going to wear it to bed."<br>"Okay."<br>"With nothing on underneath it."<br>Winking, she slipped inside, leaving him on the porch with that mental image ringing through his head </i>
</b><br><br>As for Corrado, he may seem to be the hard man on the outer surface but inside he is such a sweetheart, he was a caring brother always taking care of his EVIL sister, then a wonderful husband to Celia and even though he couldn’t do much for Maura, he still did his best. To sum up Corrado is a man of Honor; a MADE man.<br><br><b>
  <i>“But I named you Corrado… my wise, brave ruler.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>Favorite Part :</b> This kiss and every other where Corrado is present <b>
  <i> He looked down at her, curious, and barely had time to react before she sprung up on her tiptoes and forced her lips against his.<br>Every inch of Corrado, warm and sweaty, froze over like a block of ice.</i>
</b><br><br>Oh my I nearly threw my panties of the window<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414504683ra/11660758.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did not work?</b> More like a question I had, Celia is the daughter of that Mafia man who is constantly facing danger and affront men who attack him and his family. I wanted to know why he never made Celia too defense classes, why Celia has to depend on someone else to defend herself.<br><br><b> Similar books? </b> None<br><br><b> Recommended :</b> Yes to everyone who love Corrado Moretti or anyone else. It’s not important to read Sempre/ Sempre: Redemption to read this one. If you haven’t read it till now I’ll say go ahead and grab this one because you don’t know what you are missing…<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16492010477575367142" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1069878355" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1069878355" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1069878355?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=5-stars-read">5-stars-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1069878355" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13227632687293083551"><blockquote>
  <i>"Everyone was good at something. Some people painted. Others played music. Corrado just happened to be good at murder. He accepted that. Embraced it. That was who he was."</i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414523867i/11663003._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What events shaped Corrado Moretti's life and created this singular individual and dedicated husband he is in the present? How one becomes the best hitman and fearful member of powerful La Cosa Nostra? MADE is prosaic biography of Corrado Moretti and it will give you all the answers that fans of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/102399-forever' rel='nofollow noopener'>Forever series</a> have been wai</span>
  <span id="freeText13227632687293083551" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>"Everyone was good at something. Some people painted. Others played music. Corrado just happened to be good at murder. He accepted that. Embraced it. That was who he was."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414523867i/11663003._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What events shaped Corrado Moretti's life and created this singular individual and dedicated husband he is in the present? How one becomes the best hitman and fearful member of powerful La Cosa Nostra? MADE is prosaic biography of Corrado Moretti and it will give you all the answers that fans of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/102399-forever" rel="nofollow noopener">Forever series</a> have been waiting for.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"It's not easy to hurt when you hardly feel anything anymore."</i>
</blockquote><br>Corrado's upbringing was a harsh one. No love, no understanding. Just cold and cruel reality of dysfunctional mafia family. All he ever knew was world where emotions and attachments have no place. "Kill or be killed" was the main motto he learnt to follow as he grew older. However, Corrado never pitted himself and I love that about him. I love how he always found the way to cope no matter what he encountered. And most of all, I love that author never romanticized Corrado. She showed us his true self, his deepest darkest thoughts but let readers to form their own opinion. But let me tell you something. <b>If loving Corrado Moretti is wrong than I never want to be right.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Your light is the only thing in this world not tainted by my darkness."</i>
</blockquote><br>My favorite part of this book was probably Corrado's teenage years. His beginnings in La Cosa Nostra, his attempts to live "outside the box" that he so strictly created for himself and falling in love with Boss's daughter. MADE is fascinating, captivating and overall very addictive read. The best mafia story I have ever read. I know I said the same thing about Sempre duet but all three books are spectacular in their own way. It is hard to compare them because while Forever series is emotional suspenseful family saga, MADE is memoir of true mafia member whose story you won't be able to put down once you start reading it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"No one would take what belonged to him."</i>
</blockquote><br>I'm not afraid to go as far as saying that this is J.M. Darhower at her best. No matter how much I love Sempre duet, Corrado Moretti will always be my favorite and I'm glad to say that in my eyes, Mrs. Darhower did his story a justice.<br><br><i>*ARC provided by author as an exchange for honest review*</i><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13227632687293083551" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1087490573?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1087490573" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1208663464275002595"><b>5 Forever Stars.</b>	<br/><br/>I was expecting this book to be a short novella, so imagine my surprise when I found out it is in fact a full length novel. And I’m glad it was longer than I was expecting because, people;<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388297752ra/7791007.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the previous books we got the impression that Corrado and Celia’s wedding was a love match and not just a profitable mob business. In this book we find out the moment their lives entwined and never went apart again. And believe, their story is beautiful.<br/>Not only that, but we got to find out </span>
  <span id="freeText1208663464275002595" style="display:none"><b>5 Forever Stars.</b>	<br><br>I was expecting this book to be a short novella, so imagine my surprise when I found out it is in fact a full length novel. And I’m glad it was longer than I was expecting because, people;<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388297752ra/7791007.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the previous books we got the impression that Corrado and Celia’s wedding was a love match and not just a profitable mob business. In this book we find out the moment their lives entwined and never went apart again. And believe, their story is beautiful.<br>Not only that, but we got to find out how a little boy with a broken past, becomes one successful self-made man and the most dangerous mafia killer. <br>So breath deeply for a few seconds (you’ll need it), grab some tissues (you’ll also need it) and get ready for one amazing emotional roller-coaster that you’ll never be able to forget. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 5 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> I’m going t be short because I’m probably biased since I loved all the other books in this series and I jumped into this knowing that I would love it too. And I did. <br>It can be read as a standalone, (although toward the end you’ll have some spoilers on the others books) so, either you’re a fan of Sempre, or if you’re just a fan of awesome mob books or if you’re just a fan of epic love stories that surpassed every obstacle, you have to read this. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> If you loved Corrado in the previous, you’re going to love him now. He’s a killer, he’s not a good man and he’s relentless… but his amazing capacity of loving redeems him completely and you can’t help but loving him. Celia is probably the most loyal and strongest heroine I’ve ever read about. I loved her. It was also amazing to learn more about Vincent and Maura’s story. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Meh. <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Well… regarding his story with Celia, yes, they have an amazing love story. For the rest… he is a mob killer, after all. And as he said, mob guys live on borrowed time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1069783707" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1069783707" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1069783707?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23370948-arianna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23370948-arianna?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1069783707" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4152706733888543745"><b>5++++ STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414584576i/11668648.jpg' width='400' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Everyone was good at something. Some people painted. Others played music. Corrado just happened to be good at murder. He accepted that. Embraced it. That was who he was. The Kevlar Killer.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414584576i/11668649._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To say that I loved this book will be a big understatement. I loved, loved everything about it! I can’t describe in words how much I loved it. The writing, the storyline, the characters, everything was perfect. I couldn’t put it down. I devoured it! I loved every single word, chapter, p</span>
  <span id="freeText4152706733888543745" style="display:none"><b>5++++ STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414584576i/11668648.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Everyone was good at something. Some people painted. Others played music. Corrado just happened to be good at murder. He accepted that. Embraced it. That was who he was. The Kevlar Killer.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414584576i/11668649._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To say that I loved this book will be a big understatement. I loved, loved everything about it! I can’t describe in words how much I loved it. The writing, the storyline, the characters, everything was perfect. I couldn’t put it down. I devoured it! I loved every single word, chapter, part of this book. <br><br><i>“MADE”</i> wasn’t my first book who presents this dark, but fascinating world of mafia, but is the one that I loved most. It was the best!<br> <br>Reading <i>“Forever”</i> Series by this author, I was intrigued like everyone else by one character in particular – Corrado Moretti. A complex man. A dark man. The Kevlar Killer. <br><br>This book presents Corrado’s life from childhood to adulthood and it’s structured in five parts, each part representing a new stage in Corrado’s life. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"What made you this way?" <br>"Sweetheart, I wouldn't even know where to begin.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The story starts with Corrado’s childhood, where Corrado is just a lonely boy who wants and needs love. What he gets instead is a broken family who doesn’t care for him and who doesn’t understand him – a alcoholic mother who abuse him mentally and physically and an absent father.<br><br>Corrado enters in the mafia world from a young age, when he sees what his father does for La Cosa Nostra. He sees how powerful and respected his father is and he wants to be the same. It's the only think he knows. He starts his “career” in La Cosa Nostra running errands and delivering packages for only a few dollars, but he’s determined to prove his father and everyone else that he‘s capable to do his job, that he’s capable to do more, to become more. <br><br>And he does, discovering what he is best at, practically his purpose in life, becoming <b>The Kevlar Killer</b>. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Killing, to Corrado, had always been a job. It was technical, methodic. It was never emotional.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414586386i/11668754._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are many scenes where we can see how organized things are in La Cosa Nostra and how Corrado proves that he’s the best. He’s loyal for his “second family” and hardworking, becoming what he wanted - fearless, respected, powerful. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414586817i/11668786.jpg" width="400" height="530" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story also presents Corrado’s relationship and later, his marriage with Celia. They met when they were children, when Corrado and his sister come to live with Celia’s family for a short time. Their paths cross later when they are 17, when Corrado works for the boss, Celia’s father. Celia wants to be with him, but at first Corrado doesn’t think it’s possible. He fears for his life. They start to see each other despite the fact the boss is not too happy with their relationship. They can’t stay away from each other, they are too drawn to each other.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He'd never seen anything so downright beautiful. A sense of peace fell over him, calming him, pacifying the always-tense nerves inside of him, and soothing his very soul. He wanted to take that moment, to capture it, and keep it forever.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Corrado doesn’t understand how Celia wants to be with a man like him, a dark man, a heartless man, a monster, but Celia sees in him goodness, a man who cares, a man who has a heart.<br><br>Celia becomes Corrado’s only weakness, the only light in his life, his only love. He comes alive only when she’s present.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414587226i/11668803.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Celia is perfect for Corrado, she’s his match. She’s calculating and manipulative when she wants something, she's carefree and I loved her. I really loved how smitten Corrado was with her and how she had him wrapped around her finger. <br><br>Corrado and Celia’s relationship was absolutely amazing - beautiful, powerful, real. Through the years nothing changed for them, they still love each other, they care for each other, they support each other.<br><br>I loved how Corrado tried to protect Celia from the Mafia world, even if Celia is familiar and how he tried to be an involved family man. I loved how he loves her – with all his heart, unconditionally, no matter what.<br><br>Like Celia, I saw "Corrado’s heart" too. He’s a killer, but he’s not a bad man. I know how this sounds, but it’s how I really felt. He proves it in this book and in <i>"Forever"</i> Series too.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414587226i/11668804.png" width="400" height="530" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was an amazing book. One of the best I read so far. It was what I expected from this author. Corrado’s characters is developed so well. You get to know him as the Kevlar Killer, but also as a friend, husband and uncle. I loved the fact that his only weakness was Celia. Celia was amazing, my kind of heroine, actually. She’s what Corrado’s needs and she’s perfect for him.<br><br>There are many secondary characters. One of them is Vincent ( or Vincenzo ), Celia’s brother and Corrado’s brother in law. He’s presented very different from <i>“Forever”</i> series and I enjoyed reading about him and about his relationship with Maura. Poor Maura! My heart once again broke from her. <br><br>As always, the writing was perfect and it felt real.<br><br><i>“MADE”</i> was a long read, longer even than <i>“Sempre”</i>, but it didn’t felt long for one minute. Captivating, with a charming hero that will make you swoon, this book will definitely capture your attention from the start.<br><br>What an amazing, outstanding read! I can’t recommend this highly enough! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414587481i/11668847.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"The world made me this way. And maybe they all hate me, but still, they need me. Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="4152706733888543745" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57066129-aurelia?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57066129-aurelia?shelf=amazing">amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57066129-aurelia?shelf=badass-heroine">badass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57066129-aurelia?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2317128572" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10795473284363264403"><b>5 Corrado Moretti stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>“She's saying Santa Claus doesn't come to our house."<br/><br/>Celia tensed a bit, realizing he had been listening. "He can."<br/><br/>"No, he can't."<br/><br/>"We have a chimney."<br/><br/>"If something comes down my chimney, I'm shooting it...especially a fat man wearing a suit.” </blockquote><br/><br/>To say that I love this book would be a huge understatement.<br/>MADE is the story of Corrado Morretti. From his childhood, to teenage years, to adulthood. We got to see what made him the man he is today.<br/><br/><blockquote>“Everyone was good at something. So</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10795473284363264403" style="display:none"><b>5 Corrado Moretti stars</b><br><br><blockquote>“She's saying Santa Claus doesn't come to our house."<br><br>Celia tensed a bit, realizing he had been listening. "He can."<br><br>"No, he can't."<br><br>"We have a chimney."<br><br>"If something comes down my chimney, I'm shooting it...especially a fat man wearing a suit.” </blockquote><br><br>To say that I love this book would be a huge understatement.<br>MADE is the story of Corrado Morretti. From his childhood, to teenage years, to adulthood. We got to see what made him the man he is today.<br><br><blockquote>“Everyone was good at something. Some people painted. Others played music. Corrado just happened to be good at murder. He accepted that. Embraced it. That was who he was. The Kevlar Killer.” </blockquote><br><br>I sympathized with Corrado, he had a horrible childhood and had to learn to grow up too fast, he was just a boy who wanted and needed love. Instead he got dysfunctional family who didn't care for him, life was hard on him, having to grow up in a household with a manipulating little sister, an alcoholic mother who was abusive and an absent father made him have to take care of him self. He was fiercely independent and ambitious from a very young age.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1513562521ra/24700474.gif" width="300" height="274" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I loved EVERY SINGLE SECOND of this book, I really did, and now I'm getting all emotional.<br>I seriously wouldn't change a single thing, I loved how beautifully flawed these characters are, my God, this book was just something special.<br><br><b>Corrado:</b>He may seem to be the hard man on the outside exterior but when you crack beneath the surface you'll find that he was just such a beautiful person. He was a caring brother always taking care of his vile, cruel little sister, and I adored how amazing he was to Celia. He just had me swooning throughout the entire book with his silent strength.<br><br> <b>Celia:</b>She was just so easy to love right away, she is a spitfire, so full of emotions and life. She had me cracking up with her sarcastic humor and banter. I really loved how she had Corrado wrapped around her finger.<br><br><blockquote>She groaned. "Then what, Corrado? What do you want?"<br>His strong hands cupped both of her cheeks as he leaned down toward her. He stared into her eyes, drinking in the devotion she—for some godforsaken reason—felt toward him. "I'm a greedy man, Celia. I want everything.”</blockquote> <br><br> <blockquote>“Smiling, Celia leaned up on her tiptoes and kissed him. She pulled back, pressing her hand flat against his chest. His heart thumped erratically against her palm.<br>"You're wrong about yourself," she said seriously. "You said you were heartless, but that's not true. I can feel it, Corrado. It's in there. And as long as it's beating, I know it's there, working overtime, and you'll never convince me otherwise.” </blockquote><br><br>I freaking devoured this book, every single page and chapter. I just couldn't seem to put it down. Saying this book was amazing just wouldn't do it justice, it was just beyond incredible.<br>Even though I know this wasn't meant to be a sad book, I couldn't help the bittersweet feeling that came with the end of the book as I was bawling my eyes out, because I just didn't want to say goodbye. This is by my favorite book of all time.<br><br><b>Thank you J.M.Darhower, I fucking love you, you are simply amazing!Thank you for creating this beautiful peace of art </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1524436096ra/25417864.gif" width="350" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10795473284363264403" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15715152438682029587" style="display:none">★★★★★5 Million Thousand Stars★★★★★<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414929163i/11705900._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Corrado Moretti</b>, cold hearted notorious Mafia man that we met in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18338465.Sempre__Forever___1_" title="Sempre (Forever, #1) by J.M. The only happy time in his childhood is when he spends a few months with the DeMarco family, where he meets carefree Celia and Vincenzo. My highlighter was working overtime.<br><br>We journey through all their troubles, with Corrado fighting to become a Made man, his relationship between him and Vincent, the dark underworld and all of the elements that make him the man he is.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1088652228" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18304563714631788816"><b>10+++ Made Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/6d0506e5-25d9-434d-bb85-866d6e4788d4_zpswfhdvzip.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427152413i/14241177.png' alt=' photo 6d0506e5-25d9-434d-bb85-866d6e4788d4_zpswfhdvzip.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/Made%20Casting_zpsupjf30h3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427153678i/14241293.jpg' alt=' photo Made Casting_zpsupjf30h3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This masterpiece deserves a review...a good one, but I just can't!! Yep, I, Vanessa Leret Bridges, known big mouth who doesn't shut up, has been stunned STUPID!! There aren't enough words in the English language to use and attempt to string together to convey just how fucking awesome this book is! That and the fact that I'm not ready to say good bye!! I finished this book over five months ago and every time that I try to write it a review, all that comes out is <i>Ahhhhhh</i></span>
  <span id="freeText18304563714631788816" style="display:none"><b>10+++ Made Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/6d0506e5-25d9-434d-bb85-866d6e4788d4_zpswfhdvzip.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427152413i/14241177.png" alt=" photo 6d0506e5-25d9-434d-bb85-866d6e4788d4_zpswfhdvzip.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/Made%20Casting_zpsupjf30h3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427153678i/14241293.jpg" alt=" photo Made Casting_zpsupjf30h3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This masterpiece deserves a review...a good one, but I just can't!! Yep, I, Vanessa Leret Bridges, known big mouth who doesn't shut up, has been stunned STUPID!! There aren't enough words in the English language to use and attempt to string together to convey just how fucking awesome this book is! That and the fact that I'm not ready to say good bye!! I finished this book over five months ago and every time that I try to write it a review, all that comes out is <i>Ahhhhhhhh!!!!!! It's just so fucking awesome! Read it!!!!!</i> Followed by lots of fan girl screaming designed for chicks half my age! <br><br>Just...wow! Corrado Moretti will go down as my #1 book boyfriend of ALL TIME!!! Celia DeMarco Moretti will go down as my #1 favorite heroine of ALL TIME!!! <br><br>I don't think JM Darhower can write a bad book. I also don't think that she meant for this to be a sad book, but at the end? I was bawling... I mean sobbing uncontrollably, because I just wasn't ready to say goodbye. <br><br>Corrado is the sweetest, most vicious, protective, ruthless, loving, bad ass, hitman that ever graced the earth!! <br><br>Ok, here are a few fave quotes. I could easily cut and paste the entire fucking book here, because I highlighted like 90% of it. BUT, I will try to control myself!! <br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>"I'd infect you with my darkness." <br>"Or maybe I'd cure you of it." <br>"You can't know that." <br>"Neither can you."<br><br>"You're worth more than a moment, Celia," he said, reaching out and grabbing her hand again. "I'd rather give you a lifetime."<br><br>"After they invited you in, after they embraced you, there was no walking away. It's a beautiful web of glorious silk, intricately woven together with deception, which draws you in like moths to a flame. But as soon as you're close, as soon as you approach, the web snatches a hold of you and refuses to let go. And once you're stuck, the black widow comes and fucks you good before eating you alive."<br><br>“Nice job, Moretti.” Corrado shook his head. “A job is a job, sir. If you’re doing it right, there’s nothing nice about it.”<br><br>"I'll never deserve you, I'll never be good for you, but I'll spend the rest of my life trying to be enough . And the simple fact that you're letting me proves your beauty.<br><br>Her eyebrows rose in challenge. "Absurd? Tell me… when did you fall in love with me? Because I loved you the first time I heard your voice, and I don't think that's absurd."<br><br>"The world treats me like I wronged them, when really, the world wronged me," Corrado said. "The world made me this way. And maybe they all hate me, but still, they need me. Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes."</i></b><br><br>And my very favorite, because if there is one single line that sums this book up and what it's about, this is the one...<br><br><b><i>"He hated being bad for the only good thing in his life."</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>And OMG, the scene where Celia asks for the glass of water, has got to be my favorite scene in a book EVER!! I think I've read it nothing short of 100 times. It's the perfect blend of sexy and hilarious, intense and passionate! <br><br>I really have to say, If you are a lover of romantic suspense and/or mafia romance and have not yet read the Sempre series, you are seriously missing out! I will never have enough words to accurately describe how wonderful this series was, and how special all of these characters have become to me. &lt;3 It ruined me for other books. It raised the bar. It's books like these that are the reason that I read. <br><br>What else can I say here, except...<br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/tumblr_ms7gvq1iqF1sxv3djo1_500_zpsu667oekd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427153678ra/14241294.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ms7gvq1iqF1sxv3djo1_500_zpsu667oekd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

</a><br/><br/>I love Corrado and I've grew attached to all the characters. The story was gripping but I did have a few issues. There wasn't enough romance, the book was too sad and depressing and also Celia wasn't in the book enough.<br/><br/>Nonetheless I still enjoyed the majority of the book (also Ive decided to pretend I didnt read the last paragraph). This is most definitely one of the better books I've read all year. I would absolutely recommend!<br/><br/><i>Book details: standalone (recommend to read after Sempre </i></span>

This is most definitely one of the better books I've read all year.
