        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1069727340" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6618225569228337785"><b> 5+++ <i>Bellissima</i> STARS</b><br/><br/>I could have <b>lived in this book forever</b>; living every hour, minute, second of their lives. I’m real sad right now knowing that it’s over. This was a long read but it didn’t feel like it. In fact, I’m thrilled that Ms. Darhower gave us as much as she did. <br/><br/><b>“Life, he thought, had been like a line of dominos, set up in a complex interweaving path, toppling one another as things fell into place.”</b><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/sWgvDBc' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416450053ra/11968699.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Corrado Alphonse Moretti<br/><i>“Corrado…not everyone is worth as much as you.”</i></b><br/><a href='http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Corrado_zps25f3c849.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416450052i/11968696._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo Corrado_zps25f3c849.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Celia</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6618225569228337785" style="display:none"><b> 5+++ <i>Bellissima</i> STARS</b><br><br>I could have <b>lived in this book forever</b>; living every hour, minute, second of their lives. I’m real sad right now knowing that it’s over. This was a long read but it didn’t feel like it. In fact, I’m thrilled that Ms. Darhower gave us as much as she did. <br><br><b>“Life, he thought, had been like a line of dominos, set up in a complex interweaving path, toppling one another as things fell into place.”</b><br><a href="http://imgur.com/sWgvDBc" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416450053ra/11968699.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Corrado Alphonse Moretti<br><i>“Corrado…not everyone is worth as much as you.”</i></b><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Corrado_zps25f3c849.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416450052i/11968696._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Corrado_zps25f3c849.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Celia Marie DeMarco<br><i>”Your light is the only thing in this world not tainted by my darkness.”</i></b><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/CElia_zps5e86078d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416450052i/11968697._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo CElia_zps5e86078d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After having read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18338465.Sempre__Forever___1_" title="Sempre (Forever, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Sempre</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17838379.Sempre_Redemption__Forever___2_" title="Sempre Redemption (Forever, #2) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Sempre: Redemption</a>, it was perfect to finally be inside the mind of the dark and dangerous Corrdao. His story: his love and life with Celia was truly a beautiful thing despite La Cosa Nostra – This thing of ours. <br><br><b>“You’re not nervous this time, are you?” he asked.<br>“It’s the way you’re looking at me.” <br>“How am I looking at you?”<br>“Like you look at the Taj Mahal. Or the Sistine Chapel. You’re staring at me like you stare at the Mona Lisa.” <br>“I've never seen those things.”<br>“It’s like you've never seen something so beautiful before.”<br>“I haven’t.” <br><a href="http://imgur.com/FXpXpCi" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416450053ra/11968698.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>“You are worth more than a moment, Celia,” he said, reaching out and grabbing her hand. “I’d rather give you a lifetime.”</b><br><br>To have the entire story of the DeMarcos, Antonellis and Morettis told through Corrado was captivating, heart wrenching and moving. Having all the pieces come together was also so amazingly satisfying! I'll truly miss these characters. My heart aches like I'm ending things with a lover - it's not something either of us wants, it just is. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/DBMsbD5" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416450053ra/11968700.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br></span>

  </i>

</a><br/><br/>It started w</span>

<div id="review_1837845383" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1837845383" />
    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1837845383?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1837845383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer800768145091892836"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"The world treats me like I wronged them when really, the world wronged me. The world made me this way. And maybe they all hate me, but still, they need me. Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>Corrado Morretti's story is an <b>ABSOLUTE PERFECTION!</b> It's both character and plot driven as his story begins from his childhood up to adulthood. His love story, the moment he becomes a made man and earned his fame in the organized crime world as "The Kevlar Killer". Everythi</span>
  <span id="freeText800768145091892836" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"The world treats me like I wronged them when really, the world wronged me. The world made me this way. And maybe they all hate me, but still, they need me. Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Corrado Morretti's story is an <b>ABSOLUTE PERFECTION!</b> It's both character and plot driven as his story begins from his childhood up to adulthood. His love story, the moment he becomes a made man and earned his fame in the organized crime world as "The Kevlar Killer". Everything was packed with moments and made this book difficult to put down. <b>I haven't recovered from the epilogue, especially the <u>LAST PAGE</u>.</b> Gee, that one broke my heart so bad that I WEPT. I wasn't prepared for that and I don't have tissues to wipe my tears. I think I'll need a comfort food later.<br /><br /><b>Corrado "The Kevlar Killer" Moretti</b> grew up in a dysfunctional family. His mother was an abusive and alcoholic woman while his mafia father neglected him. They are truly bad at parenting as they didn't show any affections towards him, even his sister was mean to him. At a young age, he fends for survival by being part of <i>La Cosa Nostra</i>. It's been a rough journey for him to earn the name and spot in the Mafia world and he worked hard for it. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I'll never deserve you, I'll never be good for you, but I'll spend the rest of my life trying to be enough. And the simple fact that you're letting me proves your beauty. Because your beauty, Celia, is more than skin deep. As beautiful as you are on the outside -- and you are -- it's what's beneath it that's the most beautiful of all."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Though majority of this book is filled with mafia related stuff. We also get a glimpse of his love life. Believe it or not, as hot as Corrado is and women throw themselves at him. <b>Celia DeMarco</b> is the only woman who captivated him. YEP. Kevlar Killer never dated a woman in his life. They met in their childhood years and she's the daughter of his boss, Antonio DeMarco. As a ruthless Hitman, he's stern and cold-hearted but something warms him in Celia's presence. This sassy, gorgeous and fierce woman made him <i>feel</i>. She taught him how to live a little and love passionately. She <i>sees</i> him. Both good and bad. She was his light and promised she'll be his first and last woman he'll ever love. I love everything about their story. It's heartwarming, romantic and deep. <br /><br />You see, <b>Corrado isn't really a bad guy. He's a man with honor. Complex, mysterious, loyal, protective and has a good sense of judgment.</b> He kills people as ordered and he also kills people who truly deserved it. He's a man who's not afraid of death. <br /><br />Overall, <i>Made</i> is just amazing and beautifully written. I highly recommend it to Mafia Romance lovers. It's preferable to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18338465.Sempre__Sempre___1_" title="Sempre (Sempre, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Sempre</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17838379.Sempre_Redemption__Sempre___2_" title="Sempre Redemption (Sempre, #2) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Sempre: Redemption</a> first because the epilogue contains spoilers for these two books. Hands down again for J.M. Darhower! This book deserves 5 stars and if possible, even more than that.</span>
  <a data-text-id="800768145091892836" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1115888477" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1115888477" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1115888477?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1115888477" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14167573576077378121"><b>5 The Kevlar Killer Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Stop what you are doing and read Made. If you are a Sempre fan, if you are a Corrado fan, heck, if you like to read, then MADE is the perfect book for you</b><br/><br/>Sempre has been an up and down roller coast for me. I gave Sempre Redemption, two stars. I know! **Hides in the corner** BUT I did love Sempre. So I had low expectations for Made. I will be honest, I wasn’t a huge Corrado fan. I know we got a lot of him in Sempre Redemption, but let’s face it, I’m a Vincent lover (still</span>
  <span id="freeText14167573576077378121" style="display:none"><b>5 The Kevlar Killer Stars</b><br><br><b>Stop what you are doing and read Made. If you are a Sempre fan, if you are a Corrado fan, heck, if you like to read, then MADE is the perfect book for you</b><br><br>Sempre has been an up and down roller coast for me. I gave Sempre Redemption, two stars. I know! **Hides in the corner** BUT I did love Sempre. So I had low expectations for Made. I will be honest, I wasn’t a huge Corrado fan. I know we got a lot of him in Sempre Redemption, but let’s face it, I’m a Vincent lover (still am).<br><br>BUT my heart has room for one more man and that man belongs to Corrado.<br><br><b>Corrado is my book husband</b><br><br>If I had to be tied down to any mobster, it would be with Corrado Moretti. If he wanted babies, I would want babies with Corrado Moretti. I would spend the rest of my life with Corrado Moretti.<br><br>OKAY, enough, I will stop.<br><br>Made is simply about Corrado, from start to finish. Made is broken in various books (stages in his life), from childhood to present (where it leaves off in Sempre Redemption and a little after that).<br><br>It was just PERFECT.<br><br>The beginning is a bit slow because it was about Corrado’s childhood, but I had to read it. It gave a glimpse of why Corrado is who is and it will gut you! His mom is no joke crazy and it wasn’t an easy read.<br><br>My favorite part is when Corrado meets Celia and oh my goodness, I gobbled up those pages. I couldn’t get enough of it. Seeing Corrado and Celia interact is just TOO CUTE!!!!<br><br>I didn’t think I would get a full length novel, I thought this was a novella, but nope, I got the whole package and more. Made far exceeded my expectations. I was emotional, a blubbery mess and I smiled, it was just all around a joyful, delightful, intense and great read.<br><br><b>If you love Sempre, YOU WILL NOT BE DISSAPOINTED WITH MADE</b><br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23295358.Made__Forever___0_4_" title="Made (Forever, #0.4) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1412741893s/23295358.jpg" alt="Made (Forever, #0.4) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00O9YYP7W/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00O9YYP7W&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=A43VUMJFBVNBOFHN" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14167573576077378121" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1094013183" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1094013183" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1094013183?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=dark-gritty-disturbed">dark-gritty-disturbed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=criminals">criminals</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=family-friendship">family-friendship</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1094013183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3557749248012953746"><b>
  <i>*Special Corrado and Celia Valentine's story <a href='http://totallybookedblog.com/2015/02/14/tb-exclusive-last-valentines-day-a-very-special-sempre-novella-corrado-celia-by-j-m-darhower/' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a>. There's tears, bloodspill and plenty of love. God I miss Corrado!*</i>
</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423265644i/13602509.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title: </b> Made <br/><b>Author: </b> J.M. Darhower<br/><b>Genre: </b> Dark Romance (Though more of story of love than romance)<br/><b>Type: </b> Book 0.4 of Forever series<br/><b>POV: </b>Third Person<br/><b>Rating: </b>5/5<br/><br/><i><b>Note:</b> Made can be read as a standalone but do not read it before Sempre and Sempre Redemption because it contains scenes of major events in the two books. It will ruin the reading experience. But read this after those </i></span>
  <span id="freeText3557749248012953746" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>*Special Corrado and Celia Valentine's story <a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2015/02/14/tb-exclusive-last-valentines-day-a-very-special-sempre-novella-corrado-celia-by-j-m-darhower/" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a>. There's tears, bloodspill and plenty of love. God I miss Corrado!*</i>
</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423265644i/13602509.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title: </b> Made <br><b>Author: </b> J.M. Darhower<br><b>Genre: </b> Dark Romance (Though more of story of love than romance)<br><b>Type: </b> Book 0.4 of Forever series<br><b>POV: </b>Third Person<br><b>Rating: </b>5/5<br><br><i><b>Note:</b> Made can be read as a standalone but do not read it before Sempre and Sempre Redemption because it contains scenes of major events in the two books. It will ruin the reading experience. But read this after those two, it will enhance it and make you fall in love all over again with the whole family.</i><br><br>If I have to use one word to describe my feeling for Corrado Moretti it’s <b>RESPECT</b>. I love him after Sempre redemption and I love him even more now.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415113995i/11727143._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book grabbed me from the very beginning. A look at the Moretti household enough to make you understand why their lives turned out the way I did in the future. <br><br>The story chronicled Corrado’s life from the age of 7 until his adult life. We got to see how he grew up and it wasn’t pretty. He admired his father Vito even before he understood what the old man did for a living. <br><br> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You throw a man into a war and he's gonna kill, you know? Gotta do what we gotta do, any means necessary to make it out alive. And besides, people should never be punished for protecting family, no matter what."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Vito never going to get Dad of the Year award, but he was a good dad. He did what he could to make Corrado’s life better. <br><br>We also got to learn how the Moretti kids became close to the DeMarco kids – how he first met Celia and fell for her. <br><br> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"So you like my, uh, bigger places?"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I love that scene! You would only understand if you’ve read the book. I love young Celia and I love Corrado’s awkwardness with her. <br><br>He joined La Cosa Nostra in his teen as a street runner. The life wasn’t as glamorous (as what Vincent said) as it seemed. Corrado struggled to earn his place. If at first he thought it was a charmed life, not having been a made man was slowly eating him away. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407191610ra/10653380.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once he was initiated, he rose immediately to the top. Though that didn’t mean life was easy. <br><br>This book could be called Sempre: The Beginning. I love that we not only learn about Corrado’s past life, but also Vincent and Maura’s and their children. Besides all the major players in the Sempre novels, we also got to learn about the minor characters beginnings. Vincent… Vincenzo… my heart was shattering all over again for him.<br><br>The epilogue… I don’t know what to say. Was still reeling from the earlier event (again) and than that hit me. I can't... I just... I just need a hug!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407312ra/795429.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>See, all these Sempre books made me feel like the characters were my own family and this book sealed it. I laughed with them and cried for them, I would do anything for them. If people end up joining the mafia in troves after reading the series, I totally blame the author! No, the book didn’t glamorized the life (in fact it’s gritty), but it instilled in you the sense of loyalty and the value of family – that’s what it meant to be a man of honor. <br><br>I think I might have finally found my favorite male literary character. I will always love Corrado. <i>Sempre</i>. And that might be how long I would need to recover from this book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>For more reviews visit:<br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412943984i/11445453.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3557749248012953746" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1084928628" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1084928628" />
    <a title="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa"><img alt="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557708088p2/3531683.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1084928628?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" href="/user/show/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa">Spoiler Whore-Momoa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa?shelf=my-absolutely-faves">my-absolutely-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa?shelf=j-m-darhower">j-m-darhower</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1084928628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5238422601791524152"><b>MADE</b> is the long awaited story of our beloved Kevlar Killer, Corrado Moretti. <u>Who</u> makes Corrado live? <u>What</u> set the course of his life and the way he chose to live it? <u>When</u> did he know he was in in La Cosa Nostra? <u>Where</u> does everything take place? <u>How</u> did he become what he became? <u>Why</u> do certain things happen the way they happened? Everything gets answered and then some.<br/> <br/><b>MADE</b> is also the unforgettable love story of Corrado and Celia. Their love, devotion, loyalty<b><----(can't stress these enough)</b> t</span>
  <span id="freeText5238422601791524152" style="display:none"><b>MADE</b> is the long awaited story of our beloved Kevlar Killer, Corrado Moretti. <u>Who</u> makes Corrado live? <u>What</u> set the course of his life and the way he chose to live it? <u>When</u> did he know he was in in La Cosa Nostra? <u>Where</u> does everything take place? <u>How</u> did he become what he became? <u>Why</u> do certain things happen the way they happened? Everything gets answered and then some.<br /> <br /><b>MADE</b> is also the unforgettable love story of Corrado and Celia. Their love, devotion, loyalty<b>&lt;----(can't stress these enough)</b> to each other rivals all others. Corrado is his own poet. His words. His actions. Now, I've said I've swooned over some men, but Corrado blew <b>EVERYONE</b> outta the water.<br /> <br /><i>"You're worth more than a moment, Celia,"</i> he said, reaching out and grabbing her hand again. <i>"I'd rather give you a lifetime."</i><br /> <br />Corrado started to protest, but silenced his objections. Who was he to tell her what to do?<br /><br /><i>"Your light is the only thing in this world not tainted by my darknes,"</i> he said, his eyes leaving hers to rake down her flushed body. <i>"The only effect I seem to have on it is to turn it a slight shade of pink."<br />"It's because you're still looking at me that way."</i><br />He laughed lightly, his focus returning to her face, noting her cheeks growing even redder. <i>"Luna Rossa,"</i> he whispered. <i>"My very own blushing moon."</i><br /><br /><b>MADE</b> is the portrayal of the mafia family to perfection. <b>*</b>I'm no expert into the lifestyle but from other stories that I've read, this has the realistic and believable feel.<b>*</b> <br /> <br /><b>MADE</b> made me cry. The emotions that the story evoke will do you in. It did me especially, <b>ESPECIALLY</b>, at one part. Not gonna say where cause it will give it away. Let's just say that I refuse to believe it. <br /><br /><b>MADE</b> solidifies that JM Darhower has become my to go to author. Her writing and storytelling is superb. It's flawless. It's solid. <br /><br /><b>MADE is also this chicas #1 read of 2014.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5238422601791524152" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText7970048057583904195" style="display:none">I LOVED Sempre and Sempre Redemption. <span id="freeTextContainer14522958448162673565">You know you've read an amazing book when it makes you feel different ranges of emotions. I was angry, pissed, sad, happy, elated while reading this book. And I can honestly say that it was wonderful to be able to feel all those emotions, that doesn't happen often.   <span id="freeText14522958448162673565" style="display:none">You know you've read an amazing book when it makes you feel different ranges of emotions. I was angry, pissed, sad, happy, elated while reading this book. And I can honestly say that it was wonderful to be able to feel all those emotions, that doesn't happen often. You also know that the author is damn good at what she does when you fall in love with a character who's moral compass is not on the great side. Honestly, I don't even know what else I could say about this book, after I finished reading it I was at a loss for words. I just kept thinking about the ending non-stop and I still am. I don't know how another book is going to live up to this one. <br /><br />The last thing I'm going to say is that if you haven't read this book please go read it. If you haven't read this series, GO READ IT RIGHT NOW, you won't regret it. </span>

<div id="review_1069701275" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1069701275" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1069701275?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=abused">abused</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-leading-lady">best-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1069701275" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14241906318642156132">4.5 Fabulous- Heart Breakingly Beautiful Stars<br/><br/><b>"The circle of life, it’s cruel, but it’s unavoidable. If the shark didn’t eat the man, the man would eat the shark. That’s just how it goes.”</b><br/><br/>Made is the long awaited story of the Sempre bad boy Corrado. I have been such a huge fangirl over all of J.M Darhower books and Made was a perfect addition to this series!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416894444i/12103583._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>From the beginning of the story, we see Corrado struggling to survive. He isn't getting the love he deserves from his mother. His father is </span>
  <span id="freeText14241906318642156132" style="display:none">4.5 Fabulous- Heart Breakingly Beautiful Stars<br><br><b>"The circle of life, it’s cruel, but it’s unavoidable. If the shark didn’t eat the man, the man would eat the shark. That’s just how it goes.”</b><br><br>Made is the long awaited story of the Sempre bad boy Corrado. I have been such a huge fangirl over all of J.M Darhower books and Made was a perfect addition to this series!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416894444i/12103583._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the beginning of the story, we see Corrado struggling to survive. He isn't getting the love he deserves from his mother. His father is obviously up to no good. Even his sister is lacking in love and kinship with poor Corrado. He has been taught from a young age kill or be killed. One summer, everything changes for Corrado. His father is in a bit of "trouble" due to his extra curricular work activities. Corrado and his sister are swept away to stay with friends across the country. While he is there, he meets who will be the love of his life- Celia!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416894444i/12103584.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When things are safe, Corrado and his sister are swept away back to Vegas. Corrado never forgot Celia. <br><br>He begins to graduate in the ranks of the brotherhood. He is making his way to the top. He finds his place working for the big boss. The big boss, Antonio, happens to be Celia's father. Corrado is hard. He is physically able to disconnect and do what he needs to do. He doesn't question. He doesn't feel. He just does his job.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416894444ra/12103585.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Celia reenters Corrado's life, he is done for. His hard shell begins to crack and Celia works her way in. He knows that he shouldn't want her. He knows that he is no good for her. And yet, he won't let anyone else have her.<br><br><b>"She had him wrapped around her finger and he knew it right then. He knew what the ache in his chest meant. He knew why he acted so irrational. He knew why, despite everything, he couldn't be mad. He was falling for her. Hard." </b><br><br>Corrado knows that he cannot be what Celia deserves. He does his best to push her away. He knows that he cannot shield his feelings for her and maintain his working relationship with the boss. <br><br><b>"You're worth more than that," Corrado said. "You deserve to be somebody's everything, not somebody's secret."-Corrado </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416894444i/12103586.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Celia knows that Corrado is right for her. She refuses to give up. Celia pursues Corrado and her tenacity pays off. Antonio realizes that Corrado will do right by his daughter. When it comes to Celia, Corrado is a greedy man. He wants all of her and he takes her!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416894444i/12103587._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Corrado and Celia come together, it is beautiful. <br><br> <b>"I'll never deserve you, I'll never be good for you, but I'll spend the rest of my life trying to be enough. And the simple fact that you're letting me proves your beauty. Because your beauty, Celia, is more than skin deep."-Corrado </b><br><br>As we follow the relationship of Corrado and Celia, we also live through the day to day life of being a member of "the family." We experience the darkness, death, violence, and pain. Corrado is not a good man. There are many things about him that were hard to understand. And yet his love for Celia made him good.<br><br><b>"Because God knows, if He ever took Celia from me, I'd burn the world down around us all."-Corrado</b><br><br>Made is not just a love story. It is full of passion and darkness. It was a breath of fresh air to witness how everything began. If you loved Carmine and Haven than you will love reading more of Maura and the love she had for Vincent. You will treasure the good moments before things turned bad.<br><br><b>"The world treats me like I wronged them, when really, the world wronged me," Corrado said. "The world made me this way. And maybe they all hate me, but still, they need me. Because without villains, there wouldn't be superheroes."-Corrado</b><br><br>Made is such a fantastic read. The only reason I gave it the 4.5 rating instead of the 5 is because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I didn't understand why Corrado and Celia never discussed her desire to have children. I understood that they couldn't because of the life that he led. I know that he has Carmine and Haven in the future. And yet, I didn't feel like this element fit with the rest of the story. He loved Celia with everything in him. I cannot understand why he couldn't have children. In the least, I felt it deserved a moment in the story to be addressed. My heart was broken for her. He would do anything for her...and yet the one thing she obviously so desperately wanted, he couldn't give her. It left me a little broken. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Even still, Made was a special read that I couldn't put down. I loved every minute of it! <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416895310i/12104811._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14241906318642156132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1087935547" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1087935547" />
    <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog"><img alt="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514886578p2/7379751.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1087935547?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog">Gitte TotallyBookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1087935547" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2490105963959994236"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414352147i/11643662._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“What made you this way?”<br/>“Sweetheart, I wouldn’t even know where to begin.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>I have been desperately waiting to read Corrado’s story and it did not disappoint in any way; in fact it’s my favourite in this series from a pure emotional perspective. This whole series is a 5 star series but if I could, I would double those 5 stars for Made. I loved it; absolutely bloody loved it. J.M Darhower did not cut any corners; nor did she skim over any emotion or important aspect of Corrado Moretti’s life i</span>
  <span id="freeText2490105963959994236" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414352147i/11643662._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“What made you this way?”<br>“Sweetheart, I wouldn’t even know where to begin.”</i>
</b><br><br>I have been desperately waiting to read Corrado’s story and it did not disappoint in any way; in fact it’s my favourite in this series from a pure emotional perspective. This whole series is a 5 star series but if I could, I would double those 5 stars for Made. I loved it; absolutely bloody loved it. J.M Darhower did not cut any corners; nor did she skim over any emotion or important aspect of Corrado Moretti’s life in the Mafia nor his childhood leading into it. Bravo JM – standing ovation!<br><br><b>
  <i>“If we have nothing in this world, we at least have our word.”</i>
</b><br><br>Corrado’s voice was magnificent; it was powerful and not necessarily through the volume of words spoken because this man, well, is a man of few. Rather it’s through the precision and manner of his actions mostly. This man could express a thousand things through the fewest of words. When he did speak the magnitude, humour, love and the fierce straight up dry sarcasm of his few chosen words felt so incredibly powerful he took my heart in his strong hands and he took over the world. Without question this man is one of my all-time favourite anti-heroes. This man is MY hero!<br><br><b>
  <i>“People should never be punished for protecting family…No matter what.”</i>
</b><br><br>Corrado’s intrigued me since I first met him and I was already in love with him for his quiet stoicism and the power he exudes. The Kevlar Killer has a past that had me in floods of tears at only 2% into the book. Highly emotional and visually descriptive I lived and breathed his horrific childhood and youth. We learn everything there is to know about Corrado through his own voice and heart-breakingly through his Father’s, Vito.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I named you Corrado…my wise brave ruler.” “Why not Vito Junior?” “….you’re the one who made his way back.”</i>
</b><br><br>Corrado’s story is EPIC and my heart will never be the same. I LOVE LOVE LOVE this man and it’s been a while since I’ve cried so much in a story, and for no singular reason either. Many times it was the man himself; his life and how the world treats him. You’ll be pushed to find a more real, dedicated and loyal man. It’s a paradox really; Corrado is a mafia villain but you wouldn’t find a more honourable man.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Guess you found your reason to smile…”</i>
</b><br><br>The love affair between Corrado and Celia was breath-taking right from the onset. My heart felt and celebrated every step of their journey from young children to adults. There was something so honest and pure about their love, it was really quite beautiful. A stunning romance set in a violent ugly world. Celia is a brilliant heroine; brave, funny, loving and intelligent. She has a heart of pure gold.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You deserve to be somebody’s everything, not somebody’s secret.” “You’re worth more than a moment, Celia. I’d rather give you a lifetime.”</i>
</b><br><br>So, this is where it all began and what a journey it was! Time-lines are tied up and we get to experience what came before; ending up at the conclusion from Sempre – Redemption. My heart raced, broke and rejoiced. My tears flowed and my admiration sky rocketed for J.M. Darhower. Made was outstanding! I miss Corrado already; he feels a huge part of me, after all, I pretty much just spent his whole life with him and he has my heart – forever. This man loves and his love is immeasurable.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I can’t live up to it…You can’t put me on a pedestal. I’ll only fall.” ~ Celia<br>“You’ll never fall…Not if I’m there to catch you.” ~ Corrado</i>
</b><br><br>♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ <br><br><i>
  <b>*NB: In my personal opinion this series should be read in order. As Made is what came before during and after Sempre &amp; Sempre Redemption, although from Corrado’s point of view, it carries a bucket load of spoilers. It’d be a damn shame not to experience this series unspoilt!!!*</b>
</i><br><br>**Reviewed from an ARC copy provided by the author with thanks**<br><br> ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>✦✦✦<b> TB Blog :<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦✦✦ Come say Hi : <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦✦✦Follow us: <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦✦✦Check out: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a></b> <br><br><br><br>Our links for TB<br><br>Facebook<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181?ref=bookmarks">https://www.facebook.com/pages/Totall...</a><br><br>Twitter totallybooked1<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1">https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1</a><br><br>Blog<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/">http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2490105963959994236" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QuBkhqEi3fRANjUkqejbSj2tvQg/PuNjtncMp9/wCrdSIc+GsyTyixah4XwjKSR9lsYaabvvMrEwsC7qDQ+iMQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+wj1cama09uVsFxFpXMmDE58qecbrYs7CCTzDB22ooPryV5xu5z8pMMniB0vstk75RcOhp98WumO49FBz0kKBQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
